Dear friends,

we are preparing the 2-nd .NET Technologies'2004 international workshop =
and we would like to have some presentations from the MONO project and =
people active in the fields related to this.

Please, shall we ask you to distribute information on this workshop? =
Information on previous and future workshops is available at =
http://dotnet.zcu.cz=20

I enclosed the Call for papers in PDF form as well.

I thank you very much for your help and understanding.

Yours

Vaclav=20
